if (!is_file('.idea/workspace.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: .idea/workspace.xml');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('.idea/workspace.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): .idea/workspace.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') != 'e0e9bb9cac2a2161f0c839e3145ca0d9534bbcdb') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): .idea/workspace.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('.idea/workspace.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of .idea/workspace.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') !== 'e0e9bb9cac2a2161f0c839e3145ca0d9534bbcdb') {
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') !== '14d3a3ee03ab7792e2d60a27c4d7c45f91eef13d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: .idea/workspace.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('.idea/workspace.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('.idea/workspace.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('.idea/workspace.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') !== 'e0e9bb9cac2a2161f0c839e3145ca0d9534bbcdb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): .idea/workspace.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') != '2284289c390c57f3aa62e2ae92dbc40b7b511d37') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') !== '2284289c390c57f3aa62e2ae92dbc40b7b511d37') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') !== '64134fec8afadc73fe9c0bd8487fff281f39a230') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') !== '2284289c390c57f3aa62e2ae92dbc40b7b511d37') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oidplus_functions.js');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus_functions.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js') != 'dbc8536fbbef4f176e96b05810e8c219ca0f3b0c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_functions.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus_functions.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus_functions.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js') !== 'dbc8536fbbef4f176e96b05810e8c219ca0f3b0c') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js') !== '0368f1566508dded4ed9ce13aed4fdb1f4d2f321') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus_functions.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus_functions.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus_functions.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus_functions.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js') !== 'dbc8536fbbef4f176e96b05810e8c219ca0f3b0c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_functions.js');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	writefile_19();
	if (!is_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') != '4c62996ac58654538a4b55f02f0c10e1a427b49f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/includes/setup_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '4c62996ac58654538a4b55f02f0c10e1a427b49f') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '62d22b661cf7433dbd17d2eaadbec17d370a88dc') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/includes/setup_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/includes/setup_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/includes/setup_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/includes/setup_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_19();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '4c62996ac58654538a4b55f02f0c10e1a427b49f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
		}
	}
